/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar/fix_wave_D_20260413_182434/D05_slop_v3.md:594:Affine space $X = \C^3$, viewed as the local CY$_3$ total space over a point, has Beilinson quiver the Jordan quiver with three loops and cubic superpotential $W = \mathrm{tr}(XYZ - XZY)$. The critical CoHA is $Y^+(\widehat{\fgl}_1)$ (Schiffmann--Vasserot 2013). The full affine Yangian is $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at the self-dual level (Proch\'azka--Rap\v{c}\'ak 2018), verifying the five-step functor chain of Chapter~\ref{ch:toric-coha}.

/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar/audit_campaign_20260412_231034/AP17_E3_chiral.md:220:/Users/raeez/calabi-yau-quantum-groups/chapters/theory/cy_to_chiral.tex:8:At $d = 2$, the functor is unconditional: the $\bS^2$-framing of Kontsevich--Vlassopoulos enhances $\Fact_X(\mathfrak{L}_\cC)$ to an $\Etwo$-chiral algebra, and $\Phi$ is constructed end-to-end. At $d = 3$, a fundamental obstruction intervenes. The native $E_3$-structure on $\HH_\bullet(\cC)$ restricts to \emph{symmetric} braiding under Dunn additivity; the nonsymmetric quantum group braiding that physics demands can only be recovered through the Drinfeld center of the $\Eone$-monoidal representation category. This chapter verifies the $d = 3$ chain end-to-end for $\C^3$, where both sides are independently known (CoHA$(\C^3) \simeq Y^+(\widehat{\fgl}_1)$ on the CY side, $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at $c=1$ on the chiral side), and sets up the quiver-chart gluing that assembles global $\Eone$-chiral algebras from local CoHA charts.

The full affine Yangian is $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at the self-dual level (Proch\'azka--Rap\v{c}\'ak 2018), verifying the five-step functor chain of Chapter~\ref{ch:toric-coha}.

The full affine Yangian is $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at the self-dual level (Proch\'azka--Rap\v{c}\'ak 2018), verifying the five-step functor chain of Chapter~\ref{ch:toric-coha}.

/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar/.claude/worktrees/agent-ad5fe44e/audit_campaign_20260412_231034/AP17_E3_chiral.md:220:/Users/raeez/calabi-yau-quantum-groups/chapters/theory/cy_to_chiral.tex:8:At $d = 2$, the functor is unconditional: the $\bS^2$-framing of Kontsevich--Vlassopoulos enhances $\Fact_X(\mathfrak{L}_\cC)$ to an $\Etwo$-chiral algebra, and $\Phi$ is constructed end-to-end. At $d = 3$, a fundamental obstruction intervenes. The native $E_3$-structure on $\HH_\bullet(\cC)$ restricts to \emph{symmetric} braiding under Dunn additivity; the nonsymmetric quantum group braiding that physics demands can only be recovered through the Drinfeld center of the $\Eone$-monoidal representation category. This chapter verifies the $d = 3$ chain end-to-end for $\C^3$, where both sides are independently known (CoHA$(\C^3) \simeq Y^+(\widehat{\fgl}_1)$ on the CY side, $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at $c=1$ on the chiral side), and sets up the quiver-chart gluing that assembles global $\Eone$-chiral algebras from local CoHA charts.

/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar/.claude/worktrees/agent-ad5fe44e/resume_20260413_165929/C10_rmatrix_xvol_consistency.md:265:/Users/raeez/calabi-yau-quantum-groups/compute/audit/beilinson_audit_vol3_preface_wave11.md:103:- **P-S2 (line 135-138, C^3 chain verified end-to-end).** "For C^3: the Jordan quiver gives Y(gl_1-hat) ~ W_{1+infty}, and the chain C^3 -> W_{1+infty} -> Rep^{E_2}(Y(gl_1-hat)) is verified end-to-end." The isomorphism Y(gl_1-hat) ~ W_{1+infty} (affine Yangian ~ W_{1+infty}) is a theorem of Tsymbaliuk / Schiffmann-Vasserot / Arbesfeld-Schiffmann-Vasserot. But "the chain ... is verified end-to-end" is stronger than a simple iso and implicates (a) C^3 CY_3 -> CoHA (Kontsevich-Soibelman, critical version), (b) CoHA = Yangian positive part (Schiffmann-Vasserot), (c) Yangian -> E_2 via R-matrix braiding. Each step is known in some form, but "verified end-to-end" is a bold claim in a preface; cite chapter number where this is carried through, otherwise downgrade to "fits together" or "is expected to hold."

/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar/.claude/worktrees/agent-ac2d12d7/fix_wave_D_20260413_182434/D05_slop_v3.md:594:Affine space $X = \C^3$, viewed as the local CY$_3$ total space over a point, has Beilinson quiver the Jordan quiver with three loops and cubic superpotential $W = \mathrm{tr}(XYZ - XZY)$. The critical CoHA is $Y^+(\widehat{\fgl}_1)$ (Schiffmann--Vasserot 2013). The full affine Yangian is $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at the self-dual level (Proch\'azka--Rap\v{c}\'ak 2018), verifying the five-step functor chain of Chapter~\ref{ch:toric-coha}.

The full affine Yangian is $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at the self-dual level (Proch\'azka--Rap\v{c}\'ak 2018), verifying the five-step functor chain of Chapter~\ref{ch:toric-coha}.

/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar/.claude/worktrees/agent-ac2d12d7/audit_campaign_20260412_231034/AP17_E3_chiral.md:220:/Users/raeez/calabi-yau-quantum-groups/chapters/theory/cy_to_chiral.tex:8:At $d = 2$, the functor is unconditional: the $\bS^2$-framing of Kontsevich--Vlassopoulos enhances $\Fact_X(\mathfrak{L}_\cC)$ to an $\Etwo$-chiral algebra, and $\Phi$ is constructed end-to-end. At $d = 3$, a fundamental obstruction intervenes. The native $E_3$-structure on $\HH_\bullet(\cC)$ restricts to \emph{symmetric} braiding under Dunn additivity; the nonsymmetric quantum group braiding that physics demands can only be recovered through the Drinfeld center of the $\Eone$-monoidal representation category. This chapter verifies the $d = 3$ chain end-to-end for $\C^3$, where both sides are independently known (CoHA$(\C^3) \simeq Y^+(\widehat{\fgl}_1)$ on the CY side, $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at $c=1$ on the chiral side), and sets up the quiver-chart gluing that assembles global $\Eone$-chiral algebras from local CoHA charts.

The CoHA paragraph declares CoHA "the ordered bar complex of the CY_3 chiral algebra" -- but the CY_3 chiral algebra is exactly the object that does not yet exist (AP-CY6), so this is an unconstructed-object assertion in a preface posing as theorem. The `\C^3 -> W_{1+infty} -> Rep^{E_2}(Y(gl_1-hat))` chain is claimed "verified end-to-end" with no citation.

The full affine Yangian is $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at the self-dual level (Proch\'azka--Rap\v{c}\'ak 2018), verifying the five-step functor chain of Chapter~\ref{ch:toric-coha}.

/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar/.claude/worktrees/agent-ada1745e/audit_campaign_20260412_231034/AP17_E3_chiral.md:220:/Users/raeez/calabi-yau-quantum-groups/chapters/theory/cy_to_chiral.tex:8:At $d = 2$, the functor is unconditional: the $\bS^2$-framing of Kontsevich--Vlassopoulos enhances $\Fact_X(\mathfrak{L}_\cC)$ to an $\Etwo$-chiral algebra, and $\Phi$ is constructed end-to-end. At $d = 3$, a fundamental obstruction intervenes. The native $E_3$-structure on $\HH_\bullet(\cC)$ restricts to \emph{symmetric} braiding under Dunn additivity; the nonsymmetric quantum group braiding that physics demands can only be recovered through the Drinfeld center of the $\Eone$-monoidal representation category. This chapter verifies the $d = 3$ chain end-to-end for $\C^3$, where both sides are independently known (CoHA$(\C^3) \simeq Y^+(\widehat{\fgl}_1)$ on the CY side, $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at $c=1$ on the chiral side), and sets up the quiver-chart gluing that assembles global $\Eone$-chiral algebras from local CoHA charts.

This chapter verifies the $d = 3$ chain end-to-end for $\C^3$, where both sides are independently known (CoHA$(\C^3) \simeq Y^+(\widehat{\fgl}_1)$ on the CY side, $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at $c=1$ on the chiral side), and sets up the quiver-chart gluing that assembles the global $\Eone$-chiral algebra from local CoHA data via the factorization envelope.

/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar/.claude/worktrees/agent-ada1745e/resume_20260413_165929/C10_rmatrix_xvol_consistency.md:265:/Users/raeez/calabi-yau-quantum-groups/compute/audit/beilinson_audit_vol3_preface_wave11.md:103:- **P-S2 (line 135-138, C^3 chain verified end-to-end).** "For C^3: the Jordan quiver gives Y(gl_1-hat) ~ W_{1+infty}, and the chain C^3 -> W_{1+infty} -> Rep^{E_2}(Y(gl_1-hat)) is verified end-to-end." The isomorphism Y(gl_1-hat) ~ W_{1+infty} (affine Yangian ~ W_{1+infty}) is a theorem of Tsymbaliuk / Schiffmann-Vasserot / Arbesfeld-Schiffmann-Vasserot. But "the chain ... is verified end-to-end" is stronger than a simple iso and implicates (a) C^3 CY_3 -> CoHA (Kontsevich-Soibelman, critical version), (b) CoHA = Yangian positive part (Schiffmann-Vasserot), (c) Yangian -> E_2 via R-matrix braiding. Each step is known in some form, but "verified end-to-end" is a bold claim in a preface; cite chapter number where this is carried through, otherwise downgrade to "fits together" or "is expected to hold."

/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar/.claude/worktrees/agent-ada1745e/wave2_audit_20260413_001942/B03_thm_C_bridge.md:837:/Users/raeez/calabi-yau-quantum-groups/compute/audit/beilinson_audit_vol3_preface_wave11.md:13:However, several CRITICAL and SERIOUS issues hide in the substance. The modular characteristic identity `\kappa_{\mathrm{ch}}(A_\cC) = \chi^{\CY}(\cC)` (line 28) is asserted in the preface but is exactly the content of Theorem CY-D, which is labelled PROGRAMME in CLAUDE.md (d=3 conditional on A_C existing). The "six independent paths" verification of `\kappa_{\mathrm{ch}}(K3 x E) = 3` is asserted without citation and would fail AP10 if queried. The CoHA paragraph declares CoHA "the ordered bar complex of the CY_3 chiral algebra" -- but the CY_3 chiral algebra is exactly the object that does not yet exist (AP-CY6), so this is an unconstructed-object assertion in a preface posing as theorem. The `\C^3 -> W_{1+infty} -> Rep^{E_2}(Y(gl_1-hat))` chain is claimed "verified end-to-end" with no citation.

/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar/.claude/worktrees/agent-aafc36ad/fix_wave_D_20260413_182434/D05_slop_v3.md:594:Affine space $X = \C^3$, viewed as the local CY$_3$ total space over a point, has Beilinson quiver the Jordan quiver with three loops and cubic superpotential $W = \mathrm{tr}(XYZ - XZY)$. The critical CoHA is $Y^+(\widehat{\fgl}_1)$ (Schiffmann--Vasserot 2013). The full affine Yangian is $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at the self-dual level (Proch\'azka--Rap\v{c}\'ak 2018), verifying the five-step functor chain of Chapter~\ref{ch:toric-coha}.

The full affine Yangian is $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at the self-dual level (Proch\'azka--Rap\v{c}\'ak 2018), verifying the five-step functor chain of Chapter~\ref{ch:toric-coha}.

/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar/.claude/worktrees/agent-aafc36ad/audit_campaign_20260412_231034/AP17_E3_chiral.md:220:/Users/raeez/calabi-yau-quantum-groups/chapters/theory/cy_to_chiral.tex:8:At $d = 2$, the functor is unconditional: the $\bS^2$-framing of Kontsevich--Vlassopoulos enhances $\Fact_X(\mathfrak{L}_\cC)$ to an $\Etwo$-chiral algebra, and $\Phi$ is constructed end-to-end. At $d = 3$, a fundamental obstruction intervenes. The native $E_3$-structure on $\HH_\bullet(\cC)$ restricts to \emph{symmetric} braiding under Dunn additivity; the nonsymmetric quantum group braiding that physics demands can only be recovered through the Drinfeld center of the $\Eone$-monoidal representation category. This chapter verifies the $d = 3$ chain end-to-end for $\C^3$, where both sides are independently known (CoHA$(\C^3) \simeq Y^+(\widehat{\fgl}_1)$ on the CY side, $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at $c=1$ on the chiral side), and sets up the quiver-chart gluing that assembles global $\Eone$-chiral algebras from local CoHA charts.

/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar/.claude/worktrees/agent-aafc36ad/elite_rescue_20260413_221642/L10_GR_comparison.md:364:     8	At $d = 2$, the functor is unconditional: the $\bS^2$-framing of Kontsevich--Vlassopoulos enhances $\Fact_X(\mathfrak{L}_\cC)$ to an $\Etwo$-chiral algebra, and $\Phi$ is constructed end-to-end. /Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar/.claude/worktrees/agent-aafc36ad/resume_20260413_165929/C10_rmatrix_xvol_consistency.md:265:/Users/raeez/calabi-yau-quantum-groups/compute/audit/beilinson_audit_vol3_preface_wave11.md:103:- **P-S2 (line 135-138, C^3 chain verified end-to-end).** "For C^3: the Jordan quiver gives Y(gl_1-hat) ~ W_{1+infty}, and the chain C^3 -> W_{1+infty} -> Rep^{E_2}(Y(gl_1-hat)) is verified end-to-end." The isomorphism Y(gl_1-hat) ~ W_{1+infty} (affine Yangian ~ W_{1+infty}) is a theorem of Tsymbaliuk / Schiffmann-Vasserot / Arbesfeld-Schiffmann-Vasserot. But "the chain ... is verified end-to-end" is stronger than a simple iso and implicates (a) C^3 CY_3 -> CoHA (Kontsevich-Soibelman, critical version), (b) CoHA = Yangian positive part (Schiffmann-Vasserot), (c) Yangian -> E_2 via R-matrix braiding. Each step is known in some form, but "verified end-to-end" is a bold claim in a preface; cite chapter number where this is carried through, otherwise downgrade to "fits together" or "is expected to hold."

/Users/raeez/chiral-bar-cobar/.claude/worktrees/agent-aafc36ad/wave2_audit_20260413_001942/B03_thm_C_bridge.md:837:/Users/raeez/calabi-yau-quantum-groups/compute/audit/beilinson_audit_vol3_preface_wave11.md:13:However, several CRITICAL and SERIOUS issues hide in the substance. The preface uses `\HH_\bullet(\cC) \to k[-d]` (line 21-22) for the CY trace, directly violating AP-CY2 (CY trace lives in HC^-_d, negative cyclic, not Hochschild homology). The modular characteristic identity `\kappa_{\mathrm{ch}}(A_\cC) = \chi^{\CY}(\cC)` (line 28) is asserted in the preface but is exactly the content of Theorem CY-D, which is labelled PROGRAMME in CLAUDE.md (d=3 conditional on A_C existing). The "six independent paths" verification of `\kappa_{\mathrm{ch}}(K3 x E) = 3` is asserted without citation and would fail AP10 if queried. The CoHA paragraph declares CoHA "the ordered bar complex of the CY_3 chiral algebra" -- but the CY_3 chiral algebra is exactly the object that does not yet exist (AP-CY6), so this is an unconstructed-object assertion in a preface posing as theorem. The `\C^3 -> W_{1+infty} -> Rep^{E_2}(Y(gl_1-hat))` chain is claimed "verified end-to-end" with no citation.

The native $E_3$-structure on $\HH_\bullet(\cC)$ restricts to \emph{symmetric} braiding under Dunn additivity; the nonsymmetric quantum group braiding that physics demands can only be recovered through the Drinfeld center of the $\Eone$-monoidal representation category. This chapter verifies the $d = 3$ chain end-to-end for $\C^3$, where both sides are independently known (CoHA$(\C^3) \simeq Y^+(\widehat{\fgl}_1)$ on the CY side, $\cW_{1+\infty}$ at $c=1$ on the chiral side), and sets up the quiver-chart gluing that assembles global $\Eone$-chiral algebras from local CoHA charts.
